      /**
       * use this to specify Abacus Experiments that should be logged to DFP as a CMPTST value
       * @param childId : int ID of the test to be logged
       * @param testName : string name of test is ADTK experiment config (not necessarily same as abacus name)
       * @param validToLog : boolean to verify test to be logged as CMPTST var. Usually a check that parent test is 1
       * @param childValue : int bucket value of abacus test
       * @param checkControl : boolean that DFP call should request a MARQUEECONTROL adunit.
       *    this adunit is only to be used if correctly targetted in DFP to this CMPTST.
       * @param controlValues : array of integer bucket IDs for which to use MARQUEECONTROL adunit
       *    if no values are specified, and checkControl is true, all buckets will use MARQUEECONTROL if they request a MARQUEE adunit
       *
       * @access useControlMarquee boolean true if MARQUEE adunit should be re-written as MARQUEECONTROL
       * @access child : int ID of childTest
       * @access name : string name of test in ADTK experiment config
       * @access value : int bucket of childTest
       * @access validToLog : boolean if test is to be logged as CMPTST
       * @access cmptst : string CMPTST value (childID.bucket eg 12345.1)

        this.child = childId;
        this.name = testName;
        this.value = isNaN(childValue) ? -1 : childValue;
        this.validToLog = validToLog || false;
        this.useControlMarquee = (usePathRewrite === true) && (controlValues && controlValues.indexOf(this.value) >= 0);
        this.useTestMarquee = (usePathRewrite === true) && (testValues && testValues.indexOf(this.value) >= 0);
        this.cmptst = this.child + '.' + this.value;
      }
      /**
         * use this to update URL of native marquee request i.e. adx call to get native marquee Ad
         * @param oldPath : string old path of native marquee i.e NM in URL
         * @param newPath : string new path of native marquee i.e NMTEST/NMCONTROL
       * */
      function updateNativeMarqueeURL(oldPath, newPath) {
          var adPage = marqueeAdConfig.adToLoad;
          var url = marqueeAdConfig.adCalls[adPage].url;
          var path = marqueeAdConfig.adCalls[adPage].path;
          if (url) {
              marqueeAdConfig.adCalls[adPage].url = url.replace(oldPath, newPath);
          }
          if (path) {
              marqueeAdConfig.adCalls[adPage].path = path.replace(oldPath, newPath);
          }
      }
      /* enabling client side exposure logging for experiment ID 30098
        * @param experimentId : provide experiment id that needs to be evaluated and logged
        * */
      function logExperiment(experimentId) {
          require(['abacusUtils'], function (abacusUtils) {
              abacusUtils.evaluateExperimentsAndLog(experimentId);
          });
      }
      var tests = [];
      var CMPTSTs = [];
      var useControl = false;
      var useTest = false;
      var nativeMarquee = '/NM';
      /* add parent child tests below: */
      tests.push(new ABTest(25669, "TVLY_PintWizard_Child", false, -1, true, [0]));
      tests.push(new ABTest(30098, 'Storefront_Flex_MeSo_Native_Marquee_TRVL_Test', false, -1, true, [0], [1]));
      marqueeAdConfig.updatedTargeting = marqueeAdConfig.updatedTargeting || {};
      if (marqueeAdConfig.updatedTargeting.CMPTST) {
        CMPTSTs.push(marqueeAdConfig.updatedTargeting.CMPTST);
      }
      for (var t in tests) {
        if (tests[t].validToLog === true) {
          if (CMPTSTs.indexOf(tests[t].cmptst) < 0) {
            CMPTSTs.push(tests[t].cmptst);
            if (tests[t].useControlMarquee && marqueeAdConfig.adCalls && marqueeAdConfig.adCalls[marqueeAdConfig.adToLoad]) {
                useControl = true;
            }
            if (tests[t].useTestMarquee && marqueeAdConfig.adCalls && marqueeAdConfig.adCalls[marqueeAdConfig.adToLoad]) {
                useTest = true;
            }
          }
        }
      }
      if(useControl) {
          var nativeMarqueeControl = '/NMCONTROL';
          updateNativeMarqueeURL(nativeMarquee, nativeMarqueeControl);
      }
      if(useTest) {
         var nativeMarqueeTest = '/NMTEST';
         updateNativeMarqueeURL(nativeMarquee, nativeMarqueeTest);
      }
      if(CMPTSTs.length > 0) {
        marqueeAdConfig.updatedTargeting.CMPTST = CMPTSTs.join(',');
      }
      function postMarqueeLoadedCallBack(slot) {
        if (slot && slot.selector && (slot.selector === '#hero-banner' || slot.selector === '#WizardHero :first-child' || slot.selector === '#native-marquee-image-wrapper' )) {
          var selector = slot.selector === '#native-marquee-image-wrapper' ? '#hero-banner' : slot.selector;
          logExperiment('30098');
          if (!slot.devices) {
            expads.utils.toggleCollapsedExpanded(document.querySelector(selector), false);
          }
        }
      }
      if (expads.events && expads.events.postMarqueeImageLoaded) {
        expads.events.postMarqueeImageLoaded.attachHandler(postMarqueeLoadedCallBack);
      } else if (expads.events && expads.events.postMarqueeCallSuccess) {
        expads.events.postMarqueeCallSuccess.attachHandler(postMarqueeLoadedCallBack);
      }
      return marqueeAdConfig;
    });

        require(['uitk','jquery'], function(uitk, $) {
            "use strict";
            var mobileSuppress = function() {
                var isiPad = navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i) != null;
                var isMobile = navigator.userAgent.match(/Mobile|Android|BlackBerry/i) != null;
                return (isMobile && !isiPad);
            };
            var overrideForBacktab = function () {
                //overriding the condition for mobile devices only.
                if (exitWindowConfig.backTabEnabledForMobile && mobileSuppress()) {
                    $.each(exitWindowConfig, function (key, value) {
                        if (key === "hotel" || key === "shortTermHotelOnly") {
                            exitWindowConfig[key] = "intentmedia";
                        }
                    });
                }
            };
            overrideForBacktab();
            if (mobileSuppress()) {
                exitWindowConfig.deviceEnabled = false;
            }
            if ((conditionizr.ie8 || conditionizr.ie9|| conditionizr.ie10|| conditionizr.ie11 ||
                    conditionizr.safari || conditionizr.firefox)) {
                exitWindowConfig.browserEnabled = true;
            }
            var removeObjectProperties = function(obj, props) {
                for (var i = 0; i < props.length; i++) {
                    if (obj.hasOwnProperty(props[i])) {
                        delete obj[props[i]];
                    }
                }
            };
            if (exitWindowConfig.siteEnabled) {
                exitWindowConfig.enabled = (exitWindowConfig.deviceEnabled && exitWindowConfig.browserEnabled);
                if (conditionizr.ie8 || conditionizr.ie9|| conditionizr.ie10|| conditionizr.ie11) {
                    $.each(exitWindowConfig, function(key, value){
                        if (value === "popunder") {
                            exitWindowConfig[key] = "";
                        }
                        if (key === "hotel" && value === "hotwire" && window.locale !== "en_US") {
                            exitWindowConfig[key] = "";
                        } else if (key === "shortTermHotelOnly" && value === "hotwire" && window.locale !== "en_US") {
                            exitWindowConfig[key] = "";
                        }
                    });
                }
                conditionizr.on('safari', function () {
                    $.each(exitWindowConfig, function(key, value){
                        if (value === "popunder") {
                            exitWindowConfig[key] = value + "UnfocusedTab";
                        } else if ((key === "hotel" || key === "shortTermHotelOnly") && value === "hotwire") {
                            exitWindowConfig[key] = value + "UnfocusedTab";
                        }
                    });
                });
                conditionizr.on('firefox', function () {
                    $.each(exitWindowConfig, function(key, value){
                        if (key === "hotel" && (value !== "hotwire" && value !== "intentmedia")) {
                            exitWindowConfig[key] = "";
                        }
                    });
                });
                conditionizr.on('chrome', function () {
                    $.each(exitWindowConfig, function(key, value){
                        if (value === "popunder") {
                            exitWindowConfig[key] = value + "UnfocusedTab";
                        } else if (value === "hotwire") {
                            if (key === "hotel") {
                                exitWindowConfig[key] = "popunderUnfocusedTab";
                            } else if (key === "shortTermHotelOnly") {
                                exitWindowConfig[key] = "";
                            }
                        }
                    });                });
                removeObjectProperties(exitWindowConfig, ["deviceEnabled", "browserEnabled"]);
            } else {
                exitWindowConfig = undefined;
            }

                    '<img class=\"trophy-mobile\" src=\"'+ top_customer_trophy_icon +'\" srcset=\"' + top_customer_trophy_icon2x + ' 2x,' + top_customer_trophy_icon3x + ' 3x\"></img></div>';
                var gc_msg_mobile='<ul id=\"gc-msg-mobile\" class=\"gc-msg-mobile\"><button class=\"btn-text\"><div class=\"oval-2-mobile\">' +
                    '<img src=\"'+ top_customer_trophy_icon +'\" srcset=\"' + top_customer_trophy_icon2x + ' 2x,' + top_customer_trophy_icon3x + ' 3x\"></img>' +
                    '</div><div class=\"thanks-for-being-one-mobile\">Thanks for being one of our most valued customers!</div>' +                    '</ul>';
                if($("#gc-img-desktop").length==0) {
                    $(gc_img_desktop).prependTo($(".gc_img_desktop_inline"));
                }
                if($("#gc-msg-desktop").length==0) {
                    $("#account-menu ul").prepend($(gc_msg_desktop));
                }
                if($("#gc-msg-desktop-signed-in").length==0) {
                    $("#account-menu-signed-in ul").prepend($(gc_msg_desktop_signed_in));
                }
                if($("#gc-img-mobile").length==0) {
                    $("#header-mobile-toggle").before($(gc_img_mobile));
                }
                if($("#gc-msg-mobile").length==0) {
                    $("#globalSiteNavigation").prepend($(gc_msg_mobile));
                }
            });
            uitk.publish('gc_topcust_msg',{});
        }
    });
